<user_name>Jeremy Harrington<//user_name>< Text>
Okay, so I was actually trying to go to Aloha Hawaiian barbecue next door but they were temporarily closed. I looked at the reviews and while there are clearly some fake five-star reviews on there (very American names with very American pictures, but with the kind of grammar you only get from a non-native speaker) there were enough others that I figured I'd give it a shot.

We will start with the good: 1.They are the friendliest people you will ever find in a restaurant. 2. The price paid per amount of food is quite good. A two item combo could fill up 2-3 hungry adults for $10.

The less good: The food is just okay. I ordered mushroom chicken and the house special chicken, and neither one were anything to write home about. They tasted pretty similar and there wasn't a lot of flavor in either. If you use the hot sauce, all you will taste is the hot sauce.

That said, the quality of the ingredients was reasonable for the kind of place it is, so the value proposition remains decent.

It would be a fantastic place to go if you had to feed a group of teenagers on a budget.<//Text>

< review>
This facility is poorly maintained avoid at all cost!
Do not store your property here try US Storage by the 10 Freeway (Fremont exit) or the storage across the street.

The door handle to enter the facility has been broken for over a month!

The elevators are constantly broken which takes them days or even weeks and in one case a entire month to repair.

I called the property manager and left a voicemail two weeks ago and never got a call back, I called the district manager "Tony" aka Antonio last week and he hasn't returned my call.

I tried calling the regional manager today but haven't received a call back yet.

There are major ADA violations here and nobody seems to care. This facility also recently declared that they are reducing access allegedly due to break-ins...maybe the break-ins have to do with the door handle being broken for over a month and the door being propped open with a rock?!

******** Do not store your property here try US Storage by the 10 Freeway (Fremont exit) or the storage across the street.********</review>

Daisy was consistently the only staff member I remembered encountering who was of help regarding associates at this facility. She is polite and efficient. I have to lower the review from 5 stars to 3 because after a break in I discovered there is absolutely zero surveillance on the floor my unit was located. <user_name>James Karaganis</user_name><Date>1555017491514</Date><Rating>5<//Rating>< text>
I stay at this hotel whenever I fly in on business. Clean, well-maintained rooms, very nice hot breakfast, pleasant staff. There's a Denny's right next door.

WiFi is adequate: my room tested out at a consistent 7-10 mbits/sec, plenty fast for email, browsing and some streaming video. The password worked on multiple devices simultaneously which was great.

Parking is a bit tight but workable.

My only real complaint has nothing to do with the hotel itself, but that it is in a very noisy area. Trucks, horns, sirens and loud motorcycles until the weekend hours of the morning. You know your in for it when the maids leave a couple pairs of foam earplugs on the dresser.< /text>

<Time>1533085393673</Time><pics>None</pics><text>Very nice hotel for the price, staff friendly and polite, room clean and well-maintained. King size bed which, as a tall person, I very much appreciated. Room has no microwave, but does have a refrigerator. Full breakfast available though (I had eggs and sausage, and some pretty decent coffee.) Beats the usual "Continental Breakfast" of fruit and granola bars. One very positive feature is solid Wi-Fi. For a hotel network it's great: it tested out at 23 mbit/sec down, 25 mbit/sec up, and I was able to run Duo, Hangouts, Netflix, Skype and Plex with no issues. Very happy with that. The only complaint I have is that my room (I'm sitting in it as I write this) has very few electrical outlets. If you're someone like me that has a lot of electronics, bring a power strip. < text>
For cruise travelers, particularly from/to San Pedro Port, the hotel is at a prime location. Rather than pay for parking at the port for the duration of a four plus night cruise, staying one night is more than worth a nightly rate with inclusive parking. The beds are sufficiently comfortable, though the pillows are European square and quite thick with cotton, so you may prefer your more traditional American feathery rectangle pillow or the bosum of your lover. Just kidding. But not really. Anyways, the parking for your cruise or otherwise, is quite excellent and safe... Safe enough for my Tesla. If I owned one, but I don't. But it should still say something. The TV had about 25 channels, lots of them in Espanol, and lots of them fuzzy. Eat at the Baja fish place nearby, not many more options, and an excellent one. We had no notable experience with service so cannot give more than five stars. Would stay again for a future cruise and update thereafter. Love you< /text>

< review>
I came here because our original plans fell through for accommodation and things book out quick and I was in a wedding so it just needed to be close to the venue but not super pricey being as we had a lot to do and I needed several days.
It is right off the free way however it's a left turn on a very busy road so I just went to the light ever time maybe in the off season you can make a left with out waiting forever.  But that wasn't to bug of a deal.   It isn't in the best neighborhood so I would not leave anything in your car that is visible that being said.  It has a good lit up parking lot which is nice.   Bring wish clothes I don't know if they had a shortage or what I have really long hair so usually need a towel for my hair and body yeah they are really stingy about that.  They also for two people gave us one wash cloth and one hand towel.  Was kind of annoying.  Even when we asked for them.  Fortunately I brought beach towels so we made it work.  They do have a pool and hot tub it's small but fine the ph was off by alot though it was super foggy and not very clean.  We noticed the same garbage was left on the tables and ground everyday and accumulating.   The room was fairly clean.  Not as clean as I would have liked but not to the point that we felt the need to leave just wear slippers your feet will be instantly black.  We also had to  wiped things down ourselves.   They had breakfast it was typical what you would expect only bummer is the eggs were ice cold so I don't know what happened there.  So I guess I would say If you just need a place to sleep this place will do we didn't have much time to spend here anyways which was for the best.  All in all I wouldn't stay here again for the price I wish I had picked the other place but it wasn't the worse either.  I am not sure why it has the reviews it has but I'm it's fine.<//review>

We stayed at this hotel from Dec. 31/16-Jan. 2/17.  Location was great for the area.  Staff were friendly.  Check in-out were painless, they even let us check -in 1 hour earlier because the rooms were ready.  We didn't get the rollaway bed we requested, however, the staff gladly equipped us with extra sheets and blankets to make a comfortable bed on the floor for the 5th person in our room.  We were even able to enjoy the fireworks from our rooms on New Years Eve.  Close to the Harbour at Long Beach for the Fire Works and the Whale watching and Pacific Aquarium.  Breakfast was OK.  The usual Waffle maker, bagels, mini muffins, danishes, yoghurt, cold boiled eggs.  No hot items.  Also surprisingly, they didn't have any tea bags int he room, and only had Lipton Orange Pekoe in the breakfast room.  Pool was under renovation.  Wi-Fi works great most of the time.  Limited TV channels but who cares because we didn't come to watch TV.< /review>

< Text>
The price was $80 for two beds, which is about average but the beds were nice to sleep in. They had newspapers for free, the room was large, the front desk help was a small young spanish speaking girl that was annoyed that I was there interrupting her texting or cell phone activity. She treated me like an annoyance rather than important. The heater in my room was difficult to get working, it was disfunctional. There are not rooms on the first floor, they are all 2nd and 3rd floor rooms, you have to take the elevator. It is next to a freeway intersection and so it is very noisy in the front rooms, if I stayed there again, and I may, I would pick a back room away from the street. Over all, it was just ok!< /Text>
